    % Callbacks that handle component events
    methods (Access = private)

        % Button pushed function: CalculateButton
        function CalculateButtonPushed(app, event)
            %I section

            b=app.BreadthEditField_2.Value;
            h=app.HeightEditField.Value;
            t1=app.t1EditField.Value;
            t2=app.t2EditField.Value;
            l=app.LengthLEditField.Value;
            cmass=app.CentralMassEditField.Value;
            zeta=app.DampingRatioEditField.Value;
            E=0;
            density=0;
            
            %% initial disp and velocity
            x0= app.InitialdisplacementmEditField.Value
            v0=app.InitialvelocitymsEditField.Value

            % Material selection block
            if(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Steel")
                E=200 * (10^9);%Pascal
                density=7750;%kg/m3


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Aluminium")
                E=70.33*(10^9);
                density=2712;


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Bronze")
                E=111.006*(10^9);
                density=8304;
            end

            % Length conversion 1
            if(app.DropDown.Value=="mm")
                l=0.001*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="m")
                l=1*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="ft")
                l=0.3048*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="cm")
                l=0.01*l;

            end

            % Breadth conversion 2
            if(app.DropDown_2.Value=="mm")
                b=0.001*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_2.Value=="m")
                b=1*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_2.Value=="ft")
                b=0.3048*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_2.Value=="cm")
                b=0.01*b;

            end

            % Height conversion 3
            if(app.DropDown_4.Value=="mm")
                h=0.001*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_4.Value=="m")
                h=1*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_4.Value=="ft")
                h=0.3048*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_4.Value=="cm")
                h=0.01*h;

            end

            % t1 conversion 4
            if(app.DropDown_3.Value=="mm")
                t1=0.001*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_3.Value=="m")
                t1=1*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_3.Value=="ft")
                t1=0.3048*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_3.Value=="cm")
                t1=0.01*t1;

            end

            % t2 conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_5.Value=="mm")
                t2=0.001*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_5.Value=="m")
                t2=1*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_5.Value=="ft")
                t2=0.3048*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_5.Value=="cm")
                t2=0.01*t2;

            end

            % m conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_6.Value=="kg")
                cmass=1*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="lb")
                cmass=0.453592*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="gm")
                cmass=0.001*cmass;

            end

            %Area of cross section

            area=(2 * b * t2) + ((h - (2*t2))*t1);
            app.Areaofcrosssectionm2EditField.Value=area;

            %area moment of inertia

            I= (b * (h^3) /12) - ((b - t1) * ((h - (2 * t2) )^3))/12;
            app.AreaMomentofInertiam4EditField.Value=I;

            volume= area * l;

            %Mass of rod
            mass1= volume * density;

            %Lumped Mass
            mass2=(13/35)*mass1;

            %Total mass
            tmass = mass2 + cmass;

            %Stiffness
            k=(192 * E * I )/(l^3);
            app.StiffnessNmEditField.Value=k;


            %%Value of pi
            p=pi;

            %%Natural Circular frequency
            wn=sqrt(k/tmass);
            app.CircularNaturalfrequencyradsEditField.Value=wn;
            %%Natural Circular frequency
            fn=wn /(2 * p) ;
            app.NaturalfrequencyHzEditField.Value=fn;
            %%Time period
            t=1/fn;
            app.PeriodofOscillationsEditField.Value=t;
            %%Critcial Damping
            cc=2*tmass*wn;
            app.CriticalDampingNsmEditField.Value=cc;
            %%Damping Factor
            c=zeta*cc;
            app.ViscousdampingcoefficientNsmEditField.Value=c;
            
            %%Quality factor
            Q=1/(2 * zeta);
            app.QualityFactorEditField.Value=Q;
            
            %%Damped Natural angular Frequency
            try
                wd= wn * ( sqrt(1-(zeta^2)) );
                app.DampedNaturalAngularfrequencyradsEditField.Value=wd;
                %%Damped Natural Frequency
                fd=wd /(2 * p);
                 app.DampedNaturalFrequencyHzEditField.Value=fd;
            catch ME
 
            end
            
           
            
            %Logarithmic decrement
            try
                LD= (2 * p)/(sqrt((1/(zeta^2))-1));
                 app.LogarithmicDecrementEditField.Value=LD;
                 
            catch ME
                 
                
            end
            x2=[x0,x0];
            t3=[0,0];
            count=0;
            
            if zeta<1
                for t1=0:0.0001:1000000
                    t2=t1;
                    expvar=exp(-zeta*wn*t2);
                    cosvar=x0*cos(wd*t2);
                    v0var=(v0+(zeta*wn*x0))/wd;
                    sinvar=sin(wd*t2);
                    x1=expvar*(cosvar+(v0var*sinvar));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t2;
                    if (x2(end-2)>x1) && (x2(end-2)>x2(end-3))
                       count=1+count;
                    end
                    if count ==10
                       break;
                    end 
                    
                end
            end


   
            if zeta==1
                for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    x1=(exp( -wn * t1))* (x0+((v0 * t1)+(wn * x0 * t1)));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1;
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if zeta>1
               for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    zeta1=zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta2=exp((-zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    zeta3=zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta4=exp((-zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    term1=((x0*wn*zeta1)+v0)*zeta2/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    term2=((-x0*wn*zeta3)-v0)*zeta4/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    x1=term1+term2;
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1; 
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
               end
            end
 
            plot(app.UIAxes,t3,x2)
            
            % beam damping graph
            x3=[];
            incre=int64(length(x2)/50);
            
            for j=1:incre:length(x2)
                x3(end+1)=x2(j);
            end
       
            x3(end+1)=0;
            
            x=-(pi*0.5):0.005:(pi*0.5);
            for i=1:length(x3)
                y=cos(x)*x3(i);
                
                plot(app.UIAxes2,x,y,'|','MarkerSize',25);
                app.UIAxes2.YLim = [-(max(x3)) (max(x3))];
                
                pause(0.001);
       
            end
        end

        % Callback function
        function MaterialDropDownValueChanged(app, event)


        end

        % Value changed function: MaterialDropDown
        function MaterialDropDownValueChanged2(app, event)


        end

        % Button pushed function: CalculateButton_2
        function CalculateButton_2Pushed(app, event)
            b=app.BreadthEditField_3.Value;
            h=app.HeightEditField_2.Value;
            l=app.LengthLEditField.Value;
            cmass=app.CentralMassEditField.Value;
            zeta=app.DampingRatioEditField.Value;
            E=0;
            density=0;
            
            %% initial disp and velocity
            x0 = app.InitialdisplacementmEditField.Value
            v0 = app.InitialvelocitymsEditField.Value


            % Material selection block
            if(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Steel")
                E=200 * (10^9);%Pascal
                density=7750;%kg/m3


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Aluminium")
                E=70.33*(10^9);
                density=2712;


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Bronze")
                E=111.006*(10^9);
                density=8304;
            end

            % Length conversion 1
            if(app.DropDown.Value=="mm")
                l=0.001*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="m")
                l=1*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="ft")
                l=0.3048*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="cm")
                l=0.01*l;

            end

            % Breadth conversion 2
            if(app.DropDown_7.Value=="mm")
                b=0.001*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_7.Value=="m")
                b=1*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_7.Value=="ft")
                b=0.3048*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_7.Value=="cm")
                b=0.01*b;

            end

            % Height conversion 8
            if(app.DropDown_8.Value=="mm")
                h=0.001*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_8.Value=="m")
                h=1*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_8.Value=="ft")
                h=0.3048*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_8.Value=="cm")
                h=0.01*h;

            end

            % m conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_6.Value=="kg")
                cmass=1*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="lb")
                cmass=0.453592*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="gm")
                cmass=0.001*cmass;

            end

            %Area of cross section

            area=b*h;
            app.Areaofcrosssectionm2EditField_2.Value=area;

            %area moment of inertia

            I= (b * (h^3) /12);
            app.AreaMomentofInertiam4EditField_2.Value=I;

           
            volume= area * l;

            %Mass of rod
            mass1= volume * density;

            %Lumped Mass
            mass2=(13/35)*mass1;

            %Total mass
            tmass = mass2 + cmass;

            %Stiffness
            k=(192 * E * I )/(l^3);
            app.StiffnessNmEditField_7.Value=k;


            %%Value of pi
            p=pi;

            %%Natural Circular frequency
            wn=sqrt(k/tmass);
            app.CircularNaturalfrequencyradsEditField_2.Value=wn;
            %%Natural Circular frequency
            fn=wn /(2 * p) ;
            app.NaturalfrequencyHzEditField_2.Value=fn;
            %%Time period
            t=1/fn;
            app.PeriodofOscillationsEditField_2.Value=t;
            %%Critcial Damping
            cc=2*tmass*wn;
            app.CriticalDampingNsmEditField_2.Value=cc;
            %%Damping Factor
            c=zeta*cc;
            app.ViscousdampingcoefficientNsmEditField_2.Value=c;
            
            %%Quality factor
            Q=1/(2 * zeta);
            app.QualityFactorEditField_4.Value=Q;
            

             %%Damped Natural angular Frequency
            try
                wd= wn * ( sqrt(1-(zeta^2)) );
                app.DampedNaturalAngularfrequencyradsEditField_2.Value=wd;
                %%Damped Natural Frequency
                fd=wd /(2 * p);
                 app.DampedNaturalFrequencyHzEditField_6.Value=fd;
            catch ME
 
            end
            
           
            
            %Logarithmic decrement
            try
                LD= (2 * p)/(sqrt((1/(zeta^2))-1));
                 app.LogarithmicDecrementEditField_10.Value=LD;
                 
            catch ME
                 
                
            end
            x2=[x0,x0];
            t3=[0,0];
            count=0;
            
            if zeta<1
                for t1=0:0.00001:1000000
                    t2=t1;
                    expvar=exp(-zeta*wn*t2);
                    cosvar=x0*cos(wd*t2);
                    v0var=(v0+(zeta*wn*x0))/wd;
                    sinvar=sin(wd*t2);
                    x1=expvar*(cosvar+(v0var*sinvar));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t2;
                    if (x2(end-2)>x1) && (x2(end-2)>x2(end-3))
                       count=1+count;
                    end
                    if count ==10
                       break;
                    end 
                    
                end
            end


   
            if zeta==1
                for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    x1=(exp( -wn * t1))* (x0+((v0 * t1)+(wn * x0 * t1)));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1;
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if zeta>1
               for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    zeta1=zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta2=exp((-zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    zeta3=zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta4=exp((-zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    term1=((x0*wn*zeta1)+v0)*zeta2/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    term2=((-x0*wn*zeta3)-v0)*zeta4/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    x1=term1+term2;
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1; 
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
               end
            end

            
            plot(app.UIAxes_3,t3,x2)
            
            % beam damping graph
            x3=[];
            incre=int64(length(x2)/50);
            
            for j=1:incre:length(x2)
                x3(end+1)=x2(j);
            end
       
            x3(end+1)=0;
            
            x=-(pi*0.5):0.005:(pi*0.5);
            for i=1:length(x3)
                y=cos(x)*x3(i);
                
                plot(app.UIAxes2_2,x,y,'|','MarkerSize',25);
                app.UIAxes2_2.YLim = [-(max(x3)) (max(x3))];
                
                pause(0.001);
       
            end


        end

        % Button pushed function: CalculateButton_3
        function CalculateButton_3Pushed(app, event)
            r=app.RadiusEditField.Value;
            l=app.LengthLEditField.Value;
            cmass=app.CentralMassEditField.Value;
            zeta=app.DampingRatioEditField.Value;
            E=0;
            density=0;
            
            %% initial disp and velocity
            x0 = app.InitialdisplacementmEditField.Value
            v0 = app.InitialvelocitymsEditField.Value


            % Material selection block
            if(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Steel")
                E=200 * (10^9);%Pascal
                density=7750;%kg/m3


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Aluminium")
                E=70.33*(10^9);
                density=2712;


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Bronze")
                E=111.006*(10^9);
                density=8304;
            end

            % Length conversion 1
            if(app.DropDown.Value=="mm")
                l=0.001*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="m")
                l=1*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="ft")
                l=0.3048*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="cm")
                l=0.01*l;

            end

            % radius conversion 2
            if(app.DropDown_9.Value=="mm")
                r=0.001*r;

            elseif(app.DropDown_9.Value=="m")
                r=1*r;

            elseif(app.DropDown_9.Value=="ft")
                r=0.3048*r;

            elseif(app.DropDown_9.Value=="cm")
                r=0.01*r;

            end


            % m conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_6.Value=="kg")
                cmass=1*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="lb")
                cmass=0.453592*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="gm")
                cmass=0.001*cmass;

            end

            %Area of cross section

            area=pi*r^2;
            app.Areaofcrosssectionm2EditField_3.Value=area;

            %area moment of inertia

            I= pi*(r^4)/4;
            app.AreaMomentofInertiam4EditField_3.Value=I;

            volume= area * l;

            %Mass of rod
            mass1= volume * density;

            %Lumped Mass
            mass2=(13/35)*mass1;

            %Total mass
            tmass = mass2 + cmass;

            %Stiffness
            k=(192 * E * I )/(l^3);
            app.StiffnessNmEditField_6.Value=k;


            %%Value of pi
            p=pi;

            %%Natural Circular frequency
            wn=sqrt(k/tmass);
            app.CircularNaturalfrequencyradsEditField_3.Value=wn;
            %%Natural Circular frequency
            fn=wn /(2 * p) ;
            app.NaturalfrequencyHzEditField_3.Value=fn;
            %%Time period
            t=1/fn;
            app.PeriodofOscillationsEditField_3.Value=t;
            %%Critcial Damping
            cc=2*tmass*wn;
            app.CriticalDampingNsmEditField_3.Value=cc;
            %%Damping Factor
            c=zeta*cc;
            app.ViscousdampingcoefficientNsmEditField_3.Value=c;
           
            %%Quality factor
            Q=1/(2 * zeta);
            app.QualityFactorEditField_5.Value=Q;
            



             %%Damped Natural angular Frequency
            try
                wd= wn * ( sqrt(1-(zeta^2)) );
                app.DampedNaturalAngularfrequencyradsEditField_3.Value=wd;
                %%Damped Natural Frequency
                fd=wd /(2 * p);
                 app.DampedNaturalFrequencyHzEditField_5.Value=fd;
            catch ME
 
            end
            
           
            
            %Logarithmic decrement
            try
                LD= (2 * p)/(sqrt((1/(zeta^2))-1));
                 app.LogarithmicDecrementEditField_11.Value=LD;
                 
            catch ME
                 
                
            end
            x2=[x0,x0];
            t3=[0,0];
            count=0;
            
            if zeta<1
                for t1=0:0.00001:1000000
                    t2=t1;
                    expvar=exp(-zeta*wn*t2);
                    cosvar=x0*cos(wd*t2);
                    v0var=(v0+(zeta*wn*x0))/wd;
                    sinvar=sin(wd*t2);
                    x1=expvar*(cosvar+(v0var*sinvar));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t2;
                    if (x2(end-2)>x1) && (x2(end-2)>x2(end-3))
                       count=1+count;
                    end
                    if count ==10
                       break;
                    end 
                    
                end
            end


   
            if zeta==1
                for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    x1=(exp( -wn * t1))* (x0+((v0 * t1)+(wn * x0 * t1)));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1;
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if zeta>1
               for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    zeta1=zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta2=exp((-zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    zeta3=zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta4=exp((-zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    term1=((x0*wn*zeta1)+v0)*zeta2/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    term2=((-x0*wn*zeta3)-v0)*zeta4/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    x1=term1+term2;
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1; 
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
               end
            end

            
            plot(app.UIAxes_5,t3,x2)
            
            % beam damping graph
            x3=[];
            incre=int64(length(x2)/50);
            
            for j=1:incre:length(x2)
                x3(end+1)=x2(j);
            end
       
            x3(end+1)=0;
            
            x=-(pi*0.5):0.005:(pi*0.5);
            for i=1:length(x3)
                y=cos(x)*x3(i);
                
                plot(app.UIAxes2_3,x,y,'|','MarkerSize',25);
                app.UIAxes2_3.YLim = [-(max(x3)) (max(x3))];
                
                pause(0.001);
       
            end



        end

        % Button pushed function: CalculateButton_4
        function CalculateButton_4Pushed(app, event)
            b=app.BreadthEditField_4.Value;
            h=app.HeightEditField_3.Value;
            t1=app.t1EditField_2.Value;
            t2=app.t2EditField_2.Value;
            l=app.LengthLEditField.Value;
            cmass=app.CentralMassEditField.Value;
            zeta=app.DampingRatioEditField.Value;
            E=0;
            density=0;
            
            %% initial disp and velocity
            x0 = app.InitialdisplacementmEditField.Value
            v0 = app.InitialvelocitymsEditField.Value


            % Material selection block
            if(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Steel")
                E=200 * (10^9);%Pascal
                density=7750;%kg/m3


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Aluminium")
                E=70.33*(10^9);
                density=2712;


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Bronze")
                E=111.006*(10^9);
                density=8304;
            end

            % Length conversion 1
            if(app.DropDown.Value=="mm")
                l=0.001*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="m")
                l=1*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="ft")
                l=0.3048*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="cm")
                l=0.01*l;

            end

            % Breadth conversion 2
            if(app.DropDown_10.Value=="mm")
                b=0.001*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_10.Value=="m")
                b=1*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_10.Value=="ft")
                b=0.3048*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_10.Value=="cm")
                b=0.01*b;

            end

            % Height conversion 3
            if(app.DropDown_12.Value=="mm")
                h=0.001*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_12.Value=="m")
                h=1*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_12.Value=="ft")
                h=0.3048*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_12.Value=="cm")
                h=0.01*h;

            end

            % t1 conversion 4
            if(app.DropDown_11.Value=="mm")
                t1=0.001*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_11.Value=="m")
                t1=1*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_11.Value=="ft")
                t1=0.3048*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_11.Value=="cm")
                t1=0.01*t1;

            end

            % t2 conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_13.Value=="mm")
                t2=0.001*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_13.Value=="m")
                t2=1*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_13.Value=="ft")
                t2=0.3048*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_13.Value=="cm")
                t2=0.01*t2;

            end

            % m conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_6.Value=="kg")
                cmass=1*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="lb")
                cmass=0.453592*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="gm")
                cmass=0.001*cmass;

            end

            %Area of cross section

            area=(b * t2) + ((h - t2)*t1);
            app.Areaofcrosssectionm2EditField_4.Value=area;

            %area moment of inertia

            e2=0.5*(t1*h^2 +(b-t1)*t2^2)/(t1*h+(b-t1)*t2);

            I= (((t1 * (h^3))+((b-t1)*(t2^3)))/3) - (((t1*h) + ((b-t1)*t2))*(e2^2));
            app.AreaMomentofInertiam4EditField_4.Value=I;

            volume= area * l;

            %Mass of rod
            mass1= volume * density;

            %Lumped Mass
            mass2=(13/35)*mass1;

            %Total mass
            tmass = mass2 + cmass;

            %Stiffness
            k=(192 * E * I )/(l^3);
            app.StiffnessNmEditField_5.Value=k;


            %%Value of pi
            p=pi;

            %%Natural Circular frequency
            wn=sqrt(k/tmass);
            app.CircularNaturalfrequencyradsEditField_4.Value=wn;
            %%Natural Circular frequency
            fn=wn /(2 * p) ;
            app.NaturalfrequencyHzEditField_4.Value=fn;
            %%Time period
            t=1/fn;
            app.PeriodofOscillationsEditField_4.Value=t;
            %%Critcial Damping
            cc=2*tmass*wn;
            app.CriticalDampingNsmEditField_4.Value=cc;
            %%Damping Factor
            c=zeta*cc;
            app.ViscousdampingcoefficientNsmEditField_4.Value=c;
            
            %%Quality factor
            Q=1/(2 * zeta);
            app.QualityFactorEditField_6.Value=Q;
           

             %%Damped Natural angular Frequency
            try
                wd= wn * ( sqrt(1-(zeta^2)) );
                app.DampedNaturalAngularfrequencyradsEditField_4.Value=wd;
                %%Damped Natural Frequency
                fd=wd /(2 * p);
                 app.DampedNaturalFrequencyHzEditField_4.Value=fd;
            catch ME
 
            end
            
           
            
            %Logarithmic decrement
            try
                LD= (2 * p)/(sqrt((1/(zeta^2))-1));
                 app.LogarithmicDecrementEditField_6.Value=LD;
                 
            catch ME
                 
                
            end
            x2=[x0,x0];
            t3=[0,0];
            count=0;
            
            if zeta<1
                for t1=0:0.00001:1000000
                    t2=t1;
                    expvar=exp(-zeta*wn*t2);
                    cosvar=x0*cos(wd*t2);
                    v0var=(v0+(zeta*wn*x0))/wd;
                    sinvar=sin(wd*t2);
                    x1=expvar*(cosvar+(v0var*sinvar));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t2;
                    if (x2(end-2)>x1) && (x2(end-2)>x2(end-3))
                       count=1+count;
                    end
                    if count ==10
                       break;
                    end 
                    
                end
            end


   
            if zeta==1
                for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    x1=(exp( -wn * t1))* (x0+((v0 * t1)+(wn * x0 * t1)));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1;
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if zeta>1
               for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    zeta1=zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta2=exp((-zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    zeta3=zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta4=exp((-zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    term1=((x0*wn*zeta1)+v0)*zeta2/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    term2=((-x0*wn*zeta3)-v0)*zeta4/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    x1=term1+term2;
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1; 
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
               end
            end
            
  
            plot(app.UIAxes_7,t3,x2)
            
            
            
            % beam damping graph
            x3=[];
            incre=int64(length(x2)/50);
            
            for j=1:incre:length(x2)
                x3(end+1)=x2(j);
            end
       
            x3(end+1)=0;
            
            x=-(pi*0.5):0.005:(pi*0.5);
            for i=1:length(x3)
                y=cos(x)*x3(i);
                
                plot(app.UIAxes2_4,x,y,'|','MarkerSize',25);
                app.UIAxes2_4.YLim = [-(max(x3)) (max(x3))];
                
                pause(0.001);
       
            end

        end

            t1=app.t1EditField_3.Value;
            t2=app.t2EditField_3.Value;

                E=111.006*(10^9);

            end

                l=0.001*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="m")
                l=1*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="ft")
                l=0.3048*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="cm")

            end

            % Breadth conversion 2

            elseif(app.DropDown_14.Value=="m")
                b=1*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_14.Value=="ft")
                b=0.3048*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_14.Value=="cm")
                b=0.01*b;

            end

            % Height conversion 3
            if(app.DropDown_16.Value=="mm")
                h=0.001*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_16.Value=="m")
                h=1*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_16.Value=="ft")
                h=0.3048*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_16.Value=="cm")
                h=0.01*h;

            end

            % t1 conversion 4
            if(app.DropDown_15.Value=="mm")
                t1=0.001*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_15.Value=="m")
                t1=1*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_15.Value=="ft")
                t1=0.3048*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_15.Value=="cm")
                t1=0.01*t1;

            end

            % t2 conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_17.Value=="mm")
                t2=0.001*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_17.Value=="m")
                t2=1*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_17.Value=="ft")
                t2=0.3048*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_17.Value=="cm")
                t2=0.01*t2;

            end

            % m conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_6.Value=="kg")
                cmass=1*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="lb")
                cmass=0.453592*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="gm")
                cmass=0.001*cmass;

            end

            %Area of cross section

            area=(2 * b * t2) + ((h - (2*t2))*t1);
            app.Areaofcrosssectionm2EditField_5.Value=area;

            %area moment of inertia

            I= (b * (h^3) /12) - ((b - t1) * ((h - (2 * t2) )^3))/12;
            app.AreaMomentofInertiam4EditField_5.Value=I;

           volume= area * l;

            %Mass of rod
            mass1= volume * density;

            %Lumped Mass
            mass2=(13/35)*mass1;

            %Total mass
            tmass = mass2 + cmass;

            %Stiffness
            k=(192 * E * I )/(l^3);
            app.StiffnessNmEditField_4.Value=k;


            %%Value of pi
            p=pi;

            %%Natural Circular frequency
            wn=sqrt(k/tmass);
            app.CircularNaturalfrequencyradsEditField_5.Value=wn;
            %%Natural Circular frequency
            fn=wn /(2 * p) ;
            app.NaturalfrequencyHzEditField_5.Value=fn;
            %%Time period
            t=1/fn;
            app.PeriodofOscillationsEditField_5.Value=t;
            %%Critcial Damping
            cc=2*tmass*wn;
            app.CriticalDampingNsmEditField_5.Value=cc;
            %%Damping Factor
            c=zeta*cc;
            app.ViscousdampingcoefficientNsmEditField_5.Value=c;
            
            %%Quality factor
            Q=1/(2 * zeta);
            app.QualityFactorEditField_7.Value=Q;
            

             %%Damped Natural angular Frequency
            try
                wd= wn * ( sqrt(1-(zeta^2)) );
                app.DampedNaturalAngularfrequencyradsEditField_5.Value=wd;
                %%Damped Natural Frequency
                fd=wd /(2 * p);
                 app.DampedNaturalFrequencyHzEditField_7.Value=fd;
            catch ME
 
            end
            
           
            
            %Logarithmic decrement
            try
                LD= (2 * p)/(sqrt((1/(zeta^2))-1));
                 app.LogarithmicDecrementEditField_7.Value=LD;
                 
            catch ME
                 
                
            end
            
            x2=[x0,x0];
            t3=[0,0];
            count=0;
            
            if zeta<1
                for t1=0:0.00001:1000000
                    t2=t1;
                    expvar=exp(-zeta*wn*t2);
                    cosvar=x0*cos(wd*t2);
                    v0var=(v0+(zeta*wn*x0))/wd;
                    sinvar=sin(wd*t2);
                    x1=expvar*(cosvar+(v0var*sinvar));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t2;
                    if (x2(end-2)>x1) && (x2(end-2)>x2(end-3))
                       count=1+count;
                    end
                    if count ==10
                       break;
                    end 
                    
                end
            end


   
            if zeta==1
                for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    x1=(exp( -wn * t1))* (x0+((v0 * t1)+(wn * x0 * t1)));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1;
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if zeta>1
               for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    zeta1=zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta2=exp((-zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    zeta3=zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta4=exp((-zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    term1=((x0*wn*zeta1)+v0)*zeta2/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    term2=((-x0*wn*zeta3)-v0)*zeta4/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    x1=term1+term2;
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1; 
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
               end
            end
         
            plot(app.UIAxes_9,t3,x2)
            
            % beam damping graph
            x3=[];
            incre=int64(length(x2)/50);
            
            for j=1:incre:length(x2)
                x3(end+1)=x2(j);
            end
       
            x3(end+1)=0;
            
            x=-(pi*0.5):0.005:(pi*0.5);
            for i=1:length(x3)
                y=cos(x)*x3(i);
                
                plot(app.UIAxes2_5,x,y,'|','MarkerSize',25);
                app.UIAxes2_5.YLim = [-(max(x3)) (max(x3))];
                
                pause(0.001);
       
            end


        end

        % Button pushed function: CalculateButton_6
        function CalculateButton_6Pushed(app, event)
            b=app.BreadthEditField_6.Value;
            h=app.HeightEditField_5.Value;
            t1=app.t1EditField_4.Value;
            t2=app.t2EditField_4.Value;
            l=app.LengthLEditField.Value;
            cmass=app.CentralMassEditField.Value;
            zeta=app.DampingRatioEditField.Value;
            E=0;
            density=0;
            
            %% initial disp and velocity
            x0 = app.InitialdisplacementmEditField.Value
            v0 = app.InitialvelocitymsEditField.Value


            % Material selection block
            if(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Steel")
                E=200 * (10^9);%Pascal
                density=7750;%kg/m3


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Aluminium")
                E=70.33*(10^9);
                density=2712;


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Bronze")
                E=111.006*(10^9);
                density=8304;
            end

            % Length conversion 1
            if(app.DropDown.Value=="mm")
                l=0.001*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="m")
                l=1*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="ft")
                l=0.3048*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="cm")
                l=0.01*l;

            end

            % Breadth conversion 2
            if(app.DropDown_18.Value=="mm")
                b=0.001*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_18.Value=="m")
                b=1*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_18.Value=="ft")
                b=0.3048*b;

            elseif(app.DropDown_18.Value=="cm")
                b=0.01*b;

            end

            % Height conversion 3
            if(app.DropDown_20.Value=="mm")
                h=0.001*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_20.Value=="m")
                h=1*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_20.Value=="ft")
                h=0.3048*h;

            elseif(app.DropDown_20.Value=="cm")
                h=0.01*h;

            end

            % t1 conversion 4
            if(app.DropDown_19.Value=="mm")
                t1=0.001*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_19.Value=="m")
                t1=1*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_19.Value=="ft")
                t1=0.3048*t1;

            elseif(app.DropDown_19.Value=="cm")
                t1=0.01*t1;

            end

            % t2 conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_21.Value=="mm")
                t2=0.001*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_21.Value=="m")
                t2=1*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_21.Value=="ft")
                t2=0.3048*t2;

            elseif(app.DropDown_21.Value=="cm")
                t2=0.01*t2;

            end

            % m conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_6.Value=="kg")
                cmass=1*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="lb")
                cmass=0.453592*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="gm")
                cmass=0.001*cmass;

            end

            %Area of cross section

            area=( b * t2) + ((h - t2)*t1);
            app.Areaofcrosssectionm2EditField_6.Value=area;

            %area moment of inertia

            e2=0.5*(t1*h^2 +(b-t1)*t2^2)/(t1*h+(b-t1)*t2);

            I= (((t1 * (h^3))+((b-t1)*(t2^3)))/3) - (((t1*h) + ((b-t1)*t2))*(e2^2));
            app.AreaMomentofInertiam4EditField_6.Value=I;

           volume= area * l;

            %Mass of rod
            mass1= volume * density;

            %Lumped Mass
            mass2=(13/35)*mass1;

            %Total mass
            tmass = mass2 + cmass;

            %Stiffness
            k=(192 * E * I )/(l^3);
            app.StiffnessNmEditField_3.Value=k;


            %%Value of pi
            p=pi;

            %%Natural Circular frequency
            wn=sqrt(k/tmass);
            app.CircularNaturalfrequencyradsEditField_6.Value=wn;
            %%Natural Circular frequency
            fn=wn /(2 * p) ;
            app.NaturalfrequencyHzEditField_6.Value=fn;
            %%Time period
            t=1/fn;
            app.PeriodofOscillationsEditField_6.Value=t;
            %%Critcial Damping
            cc=2*tmass*wn;
            app.CriticalDampingNsmEditField_6.Value=cc;
            %%Damping Factor
            c=zeta*cc;
            app.ViscousdampingcoefficientNsmEditField_6.Value=c;
           
            %%Quality factor
            Q=1/(2 * zeta);
            app.QualityFactorEditField_8.Value=Q;
           

             %%Damped Natural angular Frequency
            try
                wd= wn * ( sqrt(1-(zeta^2)) );
                app.DampedNaturalAngularfrequencyradsEditField_6.Value=wd;
                %%Damped Natural Frequency
                fd=wd /(2 * p);
                 app.DampedNaturalFrequencyHzEditField_8.Value=fd;
            catch ME
 
            end
            
           
            
            %Logarithmic decrement
            try
                LD= (2 * p)/(sqrt((1/(zeta^2))-1));
                 app.LogarithmicDecrementEditField_8.Value=LD;
                 
            catch ME
                 
                
            end
            
            x2=[x0,x0];
            t3=[0,0];
            count=0;
            
            if zeta<1
                for t1=0:0.00001:1000000
                    t2=t1;
                    expvar=exp(-zeta*wn*t2);
                    cosvar=x0*cos(wd*t2);
                    v0var=(v0+(zeta*wn*x0))/wd;
                    sinvar=sin(wd*t2);
                    x1=expvar*(cosvar+(v0var*sinvar));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t2;
                    if (x2(end-2)>x1) && (x2(end-2)>x2(end-3))
                       count=1+count;
                    end
                    if count ==10
                       break;
                    end 
                    
                end
            end


   
            if zeta==1
                for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    x1=(exp( -wn * t1))* (x0+((v0 * t1)+(wn * x0 * t1)));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1;
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if zeta>1
               for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    zeta1=zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta2=exp((-zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    zeta3=zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta4=exp((-zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    term1=((x0*wn*zeta1)+v0)*zeta2/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    term2=((-x0*wn*zeta3)-v0)*zeta4/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    x1=term1+term2;
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1; 
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
               end
            end
    
            
            plot(app.UIAxes_11,t3,x2)
            
            
            % beam damping graph
            x3=[];
            incre=int64(length(x2)/50);
            
            for j=1:incre:length(x2)
                x3(end+1)=x2(j);
            end
       
            x3(end+1)=0;
            
            x=-(pi*0.5):0.005:(pi*0.5);
            for i=1:length(x3)
                y=cos(x)*x3(i);
                
                plot(app.UIAxes2_6,x,y,'|','MarkerSize',25);
                app.UIAxes2_6.YLim = [-(max(x3)) (max(x3))];
                
                pause(0.001);
       
            end

        end

        % Button pushed function: CalculateButton_7
        function CalculateButton_7Pushed(app, event)
            area=app.AreaofcrosssectionEditField_7.Value;
            I=app.AreaMomentofInertiaEditField_7.Value;
            l=app.LengthLEditField.Value;
            cmass=app.CentralMassEditField.Value;
            zeta=app.DampingRatioEditField.Value;
            E=0;
            density=0;
            
            %% initial disp and velocity
            x0 = app.InitialdisplacementmEditField.Value
            v0 = app.InitialvelocitymsEditField.Value


            % Material selection block
            if(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Steel")
                E=200 * (10^9);%Pascal
                density=7750;%kg/m3


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Aluminium")
                E=70.33*(10^9);
                density=2712;


            elseif(app.MaterialDropDown.Value=="Bronze")
                E=111.006*(10^9);
                density=8304;
            end

            % Length conversion 1
            if(app.DropDown.Value=="mm")
                l=0.001*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="m")
                l=1*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="ft")
                l=0.3048*l;

            elseif(app.DropDown.Value=="cm")
                l=0.01*l;

            end
             % m conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_6.Value=="kg")
                cmass=1*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="lb")
                cmass=0.453592*cmass;

            elseif(app.DropDown_6.Value=="gm")
                cmass=0.001*cmass;

            end
            
            % area conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_22.Value=="mm^2")
               area=area*0.000001;

            elseif(app.DropDown_22.Value=="cm^2")
                area=area*0.0001;

            end
            
             % volume conversion 5
            if(app.DropDown_23.Value=="mm^4")
               I=I*0.000000001;

            elseif(app.DropDown_23.Value=="cm^4")
                I=I*0.000001;

            end
            
            volume= area * l;

            %Mass of rod
            mass1= volume * density;

            %Lumped Mass
            mass2=(13/35)*mass1;

            %Total mass
            tmass = mass2 + cmass;

            %Stiffness
            k=(192 * E * I )/(l^3);
            app.StiffnessNmEditField_2.Value=k;


            %%Value of pi
            p=pi;

            %%Natural Circular frequency
            wn=sqrt(k/tmass);
            app.CircularNaturalfrequencyradsEditField_7.Value=wn;
            %%Natural Circular frequency
            fn=wn /(2 * p) ;
            app.NaturalfrequencyHzEditField_7.Value=fn;
            %%Time period
            t=1/fn;
            app.PeriodofOscillationsEditField_7.Value=t;
            %%Critcial Damping
            cc=2*tmass*wn;
            app.CriticalDampingNsmEditField_7.Value=cc;
            %%Damping Factor
            c=zeta*cc;
            app.ViscousdampingcoefficientNsmEditField_7.Value=c;
            
            %%Quality factor
            Q=1/(2 * zeta);
            app.QualityFactorEditField_9.Value=Q;
           
            
             %%Damped Natural angular Frequency
            try
                wd= wn * ( sqrt(1-(zeta^2)) );
                app.DampedNaturalAngularfrequencyradsEditField_7.Value=wd;
                %%Damped Natural Frequency
                fd=wd /(2 * p);
                 app.DampedNaturalFrequencyHzEditField_9.Value=fd;
            catch ME
 
            end
            
           
            
            %Logarithmic decrement
            try
                LD= (2 * p)/(sqrt((1/(zeta^2))-1));
                 app.LogarithmicDecrementEditField_9.Value=LD;
                 
            catch ME
                 
                
            end
            
            x2=[x0,x0];
            t3=[0,0];
            count=0;
            
            if zeta<1
                for t1=0:0.00001:1000000
                    t2=t1;
                    expvar=exp(-zeta*wn*t2);
                    cosvar=x0*cos(wd*t2);
                    v0var=(v0+(zeta*wn*x0))/wd;
                    sinvar=sin(wd*t2);
                    x1=expvar*(cosvar+(v0var*sinvar));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t2;
                    if (x2(end-2)>x1) && (x2(end-2)>x2(end-3))
                       count=1+count;
                    end
                    if count ==10
                       break;
                    end 
                    
                end
            end


   
            if zeta==1
                for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    x1=(exp( -wn * t1))* (x0+((v0 * t1)+(wn * x0 * t1)));
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1;
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
                end
            end
            
            if zeta>1
               for t1=0:0.0001:100000
                    zeta1=zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta2=exp((-zeta+((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    zeta3=zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5;
                    zeta4=exp((-zeta-((zeta^2-1))^0.5)*wn*t1);
                    term1=((x0*wn*zeta1)+v0)*zeta2/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    term2=((-x0*wn*zeta3)-v0)*zeta4/(2*wn*(zeta^2-1)^0.5);
                    x1=term1+term2;
                    x2(end+1)=x1;
                    t3(end+1)=t1; 
                    if x1<(x0/1000)
                        break
                    end
               end
            end
 
            
            plot(app.UIAxes_13,t3,x2)
            
            
            % beam damping graph
            x3=[];
            incre=int64(length(x2)/50);
            
            for j=1:incre:length(x2)
                x3(end+1)=x2(j);
            end
       
            x3(end+1)=0;
            
            x=-(pi*0.5):0.005:(pi*0.5);
            for i=1:length(x3)
                y=cos(x)*x3(i);
                
                plot(app.UIAxes2_7,x,y,'|','MarkerSize',25);
                app.UIAxes2_7.YLim = [-(max(x3)) (max(x3))];
               
                pause(0.001);
       
            end

        end

        % Value changed function: DampingRatioEditField
        function DampingRatioEditFieldValueChanged(app, event)
            value = app.DampingRatioEditField.Value;
            
        end

        % Callback function
        function ButtonPushed(app, event)
            x=-(pi*0.5):0.001:(pi*0.5);
            for z=-0.01:0.0001:0.01
                clf;
                y=cos(x)*sin(z);
                plot(app.UIAxes2,x,y);
                pause(0.0000001);
            end

            
        end
    end

Fixed beams are not allowed the vertical movement or rotation of the beam. In this beam, no bending moment will produce. Fixed beams are only under the shear force and are generally used in the trusses and like other structures. Both ends of the beam rigidly fixed with supports.</p><p>k, the stiffness of the system is a property which depends on the length (l), moment of inertia (I) and Young''s Modulus (E) of the material of the beam and for a fixed fixed beam is given by:</p><p><center>. </center></p><p><center>. </center></p><p>This Fixed Fixed beam calculator will calculate mass-spring-damper natural frequency, circular frequency, damping factor, Q factor, critical damping, damped natural frequency </p><p> It also plots the Amplitude v/s time graph for the inputs given and outputs animation of vibration of the beam</p></body></html>''}';

    % App creation and deletion
    methods (Access = public)

        % Construct app
        function app = ME352_FFBEAMCalc8

            % Create UIFigure and components
            createComponents(app)

            % Register the app with App Designer
            registerApp(app, app.UIFigure)

            if nargout == 0
                clear app
            end
        end

        % Code that executes before app deletion
        function delete(app)

            % Delete UIFigure when app is deleted
            delete(app.UIFigure)
        end
    end
